%%***>>>text element-link:[[T9 Phase 2#Dragon add]]<<<***%%Dragon add ^ATBo4Ulr

Fire/Ice/Thunder to divebombs ^rrjAEKaN

Favor + bahamut's claw -> fire out -> boss jumps to a player + party member gets thunder 
-> dynamo + thunder out

Fire in -> spread from middle -> Iron chariot + fire out -> spread and bait out 2 black holes + thunder out
-> meet in middle for beam + fire in -> bahamut's claw -> divebombs

Favor + bahamut's claw -> fire out -> boss jumps to a player + party member gets thunder 
-> dynamo + thunder out

fire in + player gets thunder -> thunder out -> ireon chariot + fire out -> spread and bait out 2 black holes + thunder out
-> beam + fire in -> bahamut's claw + thunder out -> iron chariot + dive bomb 1 -> dynamo + divebomb 2

if the boss isnt killed at this point theres another heavensfall where you need to run around the pillar and then everything repeats from the top
 ^95cHTlaL

0 dragons - 1 and 4 

1 dragon - 2 and 4

2 dragons - 3 and C ^z9HV3jPA
